<t>CREATE TABLE strategy (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    strategy_name VARCHAR(100),
    strategy_description TEXT
);


CREATE TABLE trade (
    trade_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    strategy_id INT,
    symbol VARCHAR(10),
    entry_price DECIMAL(10,2),
    exit_price DECIMAL(10,2),
    trade_date DATE,
    FOREIGN KEY (strategy_id) REFERENCES strategy(id)
);


CREATE TABLE performance (
    performance_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    strategy_id INT,
    total_returns DECIMAL(10,2),
    max_drawdown DECIMAL(10,2),
    total_trades INT,
    FOREIGN KEY (strategy_id) REFERENCES strategy(id)
);
</t><stat>UPSERT INTO strategy(id, strategy_name, strategy_description) VALUES (1, 'Trend Following', 'Follows market trends') ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE strategy_name = 'Trend Following', strategy_description = 'Follows market trends';</stat><divider><t>CREATE TABLE strategy (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    strategy_name VARCHAR(100),
    strategy_description TEXT
);

    trade_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
